\vskip 0.05in
{\EnglishColumn{I. OBSESSION OF THE MIND}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{1.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{1}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṁ me sutaṁ — ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Thus have I heard. On one occasion the Blessed One was dwelling at Sāvatthī in Jeta’s Grove, Anāthapiṇḍika’s Park.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi — “bhikkhavo”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{There the Blessed One addressed the bhikkhus: “Bhikkhus!”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“bhadante”ti te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Venerable sir!” those bhikkhus replied.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{bhagavā etadavoca --}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The Blessed One said this:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekarūpampi samanupassāmi yaṁ evaṁ purisassa cittaṁ pariyādāya tiṭṭhati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, itthirūpaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even one other form that so obsesses the mind of a man as the form of a woman.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{itthirūpaṁ, bhikkhave, purisassa cittaṁ pariyādāya tiṭṭhatī”ti. paṭhamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The form of a woman obsesses the mind of a man.” (1)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{2.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{2}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekasaddampi samanupassāmi yaṁ evaṁ purisassa cittaṁ pariyādāya tiṭṭhati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, itthisaddo.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even one other sound that so obsesses the mind of a man as the sound of a woman.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{itthisaddo, bhikkhave, purisassa cittaṁ pariyādāya tiṭṭhatī”ti. dutiyaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The sound of a woman obsesses the mind of a man.” (2)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even one other odor that so obsesses the mind of a man as the odor of a woman.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The odor of a woman obsesses the mind of a man.” (3)}}\\

\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
{\PaliColumn{rūpādivaggo paṭhamo.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{  2. nīvaraṇappahānavaggo}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{II. ABANDONING THE HINDRANCES}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{11.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{11}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppanno vā kāmacchando uppajjati uppanno vā kāmacchando bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saṁvattati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, subhanimittaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even one other thing on account of which unarisen sensual desire arises and arisen sensual desire increases and expands so much as the mark of the attractive.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{subhanimittaṁ, bhikkhave, ayoniso manasi karoto anuppanno ceva kāmacchando uppajjati uppanno ca kāmacchando bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saṁvattatī”ti. paṭhamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who attends carelessly to the mark of the attractive, unarisen sensual desire arises and arisen sensual desire increases and expands.” (1)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{12.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{12}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppanno vā byāpādo uppajjati uppanno vā byāpādo bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saṁvattati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, paṭighanimittaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even one other thing on account of which unarisen ill will arises and arisen ill will increases and expands so much as the mark of the repulsive.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{paṭighanimittaṁ, bhikkhave, ayoniso manasi karoto anuppanno ceva byāpādo uppajjati uppanno ca byāpādo bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saṁvattatī”ti. dutiyaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who attends carelessly to the mark of the repulsive, unarisen ill will arises and arisen ill will increases and expands.” (2)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{13.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{13}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannaṁ vā thinamiddhaṁ uppajjati uppannaṁ vā thinamiddhaṁ bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saṁvattati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, arati tandī vijambhitā bhattasammado cetaso ca līnattaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even one other thing on account of which unarisen dullness and drowsiness arise and arisen dullness and drowsiness increase and expand so much as discontent, lethargy, lazy stretching, drowsiness after meals, and sluggishness of mind.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{līnacittassa, bhikkhave, anuppannañceva thinamiddhaṁ uppajjati uppannañca thinamiddhaṁ bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saṁvattatī”ti. tatiyaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one with a sluggish mind, unarisen dullness and drowsiness arise and arisen dullness and drowsiness increase and expand.” (3)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{14.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{14}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannaṁ vā uddhaccakukkuccaṁ uppajjati uppannaṁ vā uddhaccakukkuccaṁ bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saṁvattati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, cetaso avūpasamo.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even one other thing on account of which unarisen restlessness and remorse arise and arisen restlessness and remorse increase and expand so much as an unsettled mind.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{avūpasantacittassa, bhikkhave, anuppannañceva uddhaccakukkuccaṁ uppajjati uppannañca uddhaccakukkuccaṁ bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saṁvattatī”ti. catutthaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one with an unsettled mind, unarisen restlessness and remorse arise and arisen restlessness and remorse increase and expand.” (4)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{15.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{15}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā vicikicchā uppajjati uppannā vā vicikicchā bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saṁvattati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, ayonisomanasikāro.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even one other thing on account of which unarisen doubt arises and arisen doubt increases and expands so much as careless attention.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayoniso, bhikkhave, manasi karoto anuppannā ceva vicikicchā uppajjati uppannā ca vicikicchā bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saṁvattatī”ti. pañcamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who attends carelessly, unarisen doubt arises and arisen doubt increases and expands.” (5)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{16.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{16}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppanno vā kāmacchando nuppajjati uppanno vā kāmacchando pahīyati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, asubhanimittaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even one other thing on account of which unarisen sensual desire does not arise and arisen sensual desire is abandoned so much as the mark of the unattractive.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{asubhanimittaṁ, bhikkhave, yoniso manasi karoto anuppanno ceva kāmacchando nuppajjati uppanno ca kāmacchando pahīyatī”ti. chaṭṭhaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who attends carefully to the mark of the unattractive, unarisen sensual desire does not arise and arisen sensual desire is abandoned.” (6)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{17.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{17}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppanno vā byāpādo nuppajjati uppanno vā byāpādo pahīyati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, mettā cetovimutti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even one other thing on account of which unarisen ill will does not arise and arisen ill will is abandoned so much as the liberation of the mind by loving-kindness.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{mettaṁ, bhikkhave, cetovimuttiṁ yoniso manasi karoto anuppanno ceva byāpādo nuppajjati uppanno ca byāpādo pahīyatī”ti. sattamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who attends carefully to the liberation of the mind by loving-kindness, unarisen ill will does not arise and arisen ill will is abandoned.” (7)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{18.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{18}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannaṁ vā thinamiddhaṁ nuppajjati uppannaṁ vā thinamiddhaṁ pahīyati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, ārambhadhātu nikkamadhātu parakkamadhātu.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even one other thing on account of which unarisen dullness and drowsiness do not arise and arisen dullness and drowsiness are abandoned so much as the element of instigation, the element of persistence, the element of exertion.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{āraddhavīriyassa, bhikkhave, anuppannañceva thinamiddhaṁ nuppajjati uppannañca thinamiddhaṁ pahīyatī”ti. aṭṭhamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who has aroused energy, unarisen dullness and drowsiness do not arise and arisen dullness and drowsiness are abandoned.” (8)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{19.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{19}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannaṁ vā uddhaccakukkuccaṁ nuppajjati uppannaṁ vā uddhaccakukkuccaṁ pahīyati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, cetaso vūpasamo.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even one other thing on account of which unarisen restlessness and remorse do not arise and arisen restlessness and remorse are abandoned so much as pacification of the mind.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{vūpasantacittassa, bhikkhave, anuppannañceva uddhaccakukkuccaṁ nuppajjati uppannañca uddhaccakukkuccaṁ pahīyatī”ti. navamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one with a pacified mind, unarisen restlessness and remorse do not arise and arisen restlessness and remorse are abandoned.” (9)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{20.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{20}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā vicikicchā nuppajjati uppannā vā vicikicchā pahīyati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, yonisomanasikāro.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even one other thing on account of which unarisen doubt does not arise and arisen doubt is abandoned so much as careful attention.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yoniso, bhikkhave, manasi karoto anuppannā ceva vicikicchā nuppajjati uppannā ca vicikicchā pahīyatī”ti. dasamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who attends carefully, unarisen doubt does not arise and arisen doubt is abandoned.” (10)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
{\PaliColumn{nīvaraṇappahānavaggo dutiyo.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{  3. akammaniyavaggo}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{III. UNWIELDY}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{21.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{21}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yaṁ evaṁ abhāvitaṁ akammaniyaṁ hoti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, cittaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even one other thing that when undeveloped is so unwieldy as the mind.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{cittaṁ, bhikkhave, abhāvitaṁ akammaniyaṁ hotī”ti. paṭhamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{An undeveloped mind is unwieldy.” (1)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\PaliColumn{4. adantavaggo}}\\

{\PaliColumn{35.}}\\

{\EnglishColumn{35}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yaṁ evaṁ arakkhitaṁ mahato anatthāya saṁvattati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, cittaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even one other thing that when unprotected leads to such great harm as the mind.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{cittaṁ, bhikkhave, arakkhitaṁ mahato anatthāya saṁvattatī”ti. pañcamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{An unprotected mind leads to great harm.” (5)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\PaliColumn{36.}}\\

{\PaliColumn{39.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{39}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yaṁ evaṁ adantaṁ aguttaṁ arakkhitaṁ asaṁvutaṁ mahato anatthāya saṁvattati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, cittaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

{\EnglishColumn{40}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
{\PaliColumn{adantavaggo catuttho.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{5. paṇihitācchavaggo}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{V. A SPIKE}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{41.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{41}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, sālisūkaṁ vā yavasūkaṁ vā micchāpaṇihitaṁ hatthena vā pādena vā akkantaṁ hatthaṁ vā pādaṁ vā bhecchati lohitaṁ vā uppādessatīti netaṁ ṭhānaṁ vijjati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, suppose a misdirected spike of hill rice or barley were pressed by the hand or foot. It is impossible that it would pierce the hand or the foot and draw blood.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu? micchāpaṇihitattā, bhikkhave, sūkassa.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason? Because the spike is misdirected.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evamevaṁ kho, bhikkhave, so vata bhikkhu micchāpaṇihitena cittena avijjaṁ bhecchati, vijjaṁ uppādessati, nibbānaṁ sacchikarissatīti netaṁ ṭhānaṁ vijjati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{So too, it is impossible that a bhikkhu with a misdirected mind would pierce ignorance, arouse true knowledge, and realize nibbāna.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu? micchāpaṇihitattā, bhikkhave, cittassā”ti. paṭhamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason? Because the mind is misdirected.” (1)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{42.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{42}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, sālisūkaṁ vā yavasūkaṁ vā sammāpaṇihitaṁ hatthena vā pādena vā akkantaṁ hatthaṁ vā pādaṁ vā bhecchati lohitaṁ vā uppādessatīti ṭhānametaṁ vijjati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, suppose a well-directed spike of hill rice or barley were pressed by the hand or foot. It is possible that it would pierce the hand or the foot and draw blood.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu? sammāpaṇihitattā, bhikkhave, sūkassa.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason? Because the spike is well directed.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evamevaṁ kho, bhikkhave, so vata bhikkhu sammāpaṇihitena cittena avijjaṁ bhecchati, vijjaṁ uppādessati, nibbānaṁ sacchikarissatīti ṭhānametaṁ vijjati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{So too, it is possible that a bhikkhu with a well-directed mind would pierce ignorance, arouse true knowledge, and realize nibbāna.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu? sammāpaṇihitattā, bhikkhave, cittassā”ti. dutiyaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason? Because the mind is well directed.” (2)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{43.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{43}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“idhāhaṁ, bhikkhave, ekaccaṁ puggalaṁ paduṭṭhacittaṁ evaṁ cetasā ceto paricca pajānāmi — ‘imamhi ce ayaṁ samaye puggalo kālaṁ kareyya, yathābhataṁ nikkhitto evaṁ niraye’.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Here, bhikkhus, having encompassed a mentally corrupted person’s mind with my own mind, I understand that if this person were to die at this time, he would be deposited in hell as if brought there.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu? cittaṁ hissa, bhikkhave, paduṭṭhaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason? Because his mind is corrupted.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“cetopadosahetu pana, bhikkhave, evamidhekacce sattā kāyassa bhedā paraṁ maraṇā apāyaṁ duggatiṁ vinipātaṁ nirayaṁ upapajjantī”ti. tatiyaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{It is because of mental corruption that with the breakup of the body, after death, some beings here are reborn in the plane of misery, in a bad destination, in the lower world, in hell.” (3)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{44.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{44}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“idhāhaṁ, bhikkhave, ekaccaṁ puggalaṁ pasannacittaṁ evaṁ cetasā ceto paricca pajānāmi — ‘imamhi ce ayaṁ samaye puggalo kālaṁ kareyya, yathābhataṁ nikkhitto evaṁ sagge’.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Here, bhikkhus, having encompassed a mentally placid person’s mind with my own mind, I understand that if this person were to die at this time, he would be deposited in heaven as if brought there.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu? cittaṁ hissa, bhikkhave, pasannaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason? Because his mind is placid.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“cetopasādahetu pana, bhikkhave, evamidhekacce sattā kāyassa bhedā paraṁ maraṇā sugatiṁ saggaṁ lokaṁ upapajjantī”ti. catutthaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{It is because of mental placidity that with the breakup of the body, after death, some beings here are reborn in a good destination, in a heavenly world.” (4)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{45.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{45}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, udakarahado āvilo luḷito kalalībhūto}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, suppose there were a pool of water that was cloudy, turbid, and muddy.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tattha cakkhumā puriso tīre ṭhito na passeyya sippisambukampi sakkharakaṭhalampi macchagumbampi carantampi tiṭṭhantampi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Then a man with good sight standing on the bank could not see shells, gravel and pebbles, and shoals of fish swimming about and resting.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu? āvilattā, bhikkhave, udakassa.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason? Because the water is cloudy.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evamevaṁ kho, bhikkhave, so vata bhikkhu āvilena cittena attatthaṁ vā ñassati paratthaṁ vā ñassati ubhayatthaṁ vā ñassati uttariṁ vā manussadhammā alamariyañāṇadassanavisesaṁ sacchikarissatīti netaṁ ṭhānaṁ vijjati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{So too, it is impossible for a bhikkhu with a cloudy mind to know his own good, the good of others, or the good of both, or to realize a superhuman distinction in knowledge and vision worthy of the noble ones.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu? āvilattā, bhikkhave, cittassā”ti. pañcamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason? Because his mind is cloudy.” (5)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{46.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{46}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, udakarahado accho vippasanno anāvilo}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, suppose there were a pool of water that was clear, serene, and limpid.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tattha cakkhumā puriso tīre ṭhito passeyya sippisambukampi sakkharakaṭhalampi macchagumbampi carantampi tiṭṭhantampi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Then a man with good sight standing on the bank could see shells, gravel and pebbles, and shoals of fish swimming about and resting.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu? anāvilattā, bhikkhave, udakassa.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason? Because the water is limpid.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evamevaṁ kho, bhikkhave, so vata bhikkhu anāvilena cittena attatthaṁ vā ñassati paratthaṁ vā ñassati ubhayatthaṁ vā ñassati uttariṁ vā manussadhammā alamariyañāṇadassanavisesaṁ sacchikarissatīti ṭhānametaṁ vijjati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{So too, it is possible for a bhikkhu with a limpid mind to know his own good, the good of others, and the good of both, and to realize a superhuman distinction in knowledge and vision worthy of the noble ones.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu? anāvilattā, bhikkhave, cittassā”ti. chaṭṭhaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason? Because his mind is limpid.” (6)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{47.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{47}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, yāni kānici rukkhajātānaṁ phandano tesaṁ aggamakkhāyati yadidaṁ mudutāya ceva kammaññatāya ca.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, just as sandalwood is declared to be the best of trees with respect to malleability and wieldiness,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evamevaṁ kho ahaṁ, bhikkhave, nāññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yaṁ evaṁ bhāvitaṁ bahulīkataṁ mudu ca hoti kammaññañca yathayidaṁ cittaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{so too I do not see even one other thing that, when developed and cultivated, is so malleable and wieldy as the mind.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{cittaṁ, bhikkhave, bhāvitaṁ bahulīkataṁ mudu ca hoti kammaññañca hotī”ti. sattamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{A developed and cultivated mind is malleable and wieldy.” (7)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{48.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{48}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yaṁ evaṁ lahuparivattaṁ yathayidaṁ cittaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even one other thing that changes so quickly as the mind.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yāvañcidaṁ, bhikkhave, upamāpi na sukarā yāva lahuparivattaṁ cittan”ti. aṭṭhamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{It is not easy to give a simile for how quickly the mind changes.” (8)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{49.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{49}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“pabhassaramidaṁ, bhikkhave, cittaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Luminous, bhikkhus, is this mind,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tañca kho āgantukehi upakkilesehi upakkiliṭṭhan”ti. navamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{but it is defiled by adventitious defilements.” (9)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{50.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{50}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“pabhassaramidaṁ, bhikkhave, cittaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Luminous, bhikkhus, is this mind,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tañca kho āgantukehi upakkilesehi vippamuttan”ti. dasamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and it is freed from adventitious defilements.” (10)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
{\PaliColumn{paṇihitācchavaggo pañcamo.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{6. accharāsaṅghātavaggo}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{VI. LUMINOUS}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{51.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{51}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“pabhassaramidaṁ, bhikkhave, cittaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Luminous, bhikkhus, is this mind,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tañca kho āgantukehi upakkilesehi upakkiliṭṭhaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{but it is defiled by adventitious defilements.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ assutavā puthujjano yathābhūtaṁ nappajānāti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The uninstructed worldling does not understand this as it really is;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tasmā ‘assutavato puthujjanassa cittabhāvanā natthī’ti vadāmī”ti. paṭhamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{therefore I say that for the uninstructed worldling there is no development of the mind.” (1)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{52.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{52}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“pabhassaramidaṁ, bhikkhave, cittaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Luminous, bhikkhus, is this mind,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tañca kho āgantukehi upakkilesehi vippamuttaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and it is freed from adventitious defilements.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ sutavā ariyasāvako yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The instructed noble disciple understands this as it really is;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tasmā ‘sutavato ariyasāvakassa cittabhāvanā atthī’ti vadāmī”ti. dutiyaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{therefore I say that for the instructed noble disciple there is development of the mind.” (2)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{53.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{53}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“accharāsaṅghātamattampi ce, bhikkhave, bhikkhu mettācittaṁ āsevati;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, if for just the time of a finger snap a bhikkhu pursues a mind of loving-kindness,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave — ‘bhikkhu arittajjhāno viharati satthusāsanakaro ovādapatikaro, amoghaṁ raṭṭhapiṇḍaṁ bhuñjati’.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{he is called a bhikkhu who is not devoid of jhāna, who acts upon the teaching of the Teacher, who responds to his advice, and who does not eat the country’s almsfood in vain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ko pana vādo ye naṁ bahulīkarontī”ti! tatiyaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{How much more, then, those who cultivate it!” (3)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{54.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{54}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“accharāsaṅghātamattampi ce, bhikkhave, bhikkhu mettācittaṁ bhāveti;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, if for just the time of a finger snap a bhikkhu develops a mind of loving-kindness,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave — ‘bhikkhu arittajjhāno viharati satthusāsanakaro ovādapatikaro, amoghaṁ raṭṭhapiṇḍaṁ bhuñjati’.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{he is called a bhikkhu who is not devoid of jhāna, who acts upon the teaching of the Teacher, who responds to his advice, and who does not eat the country’s almsfood in vain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ko pana vādo ye naṁ bahulīkarontī”ti! catutthaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{How much more, then, those who cultivate it!” (4)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{55.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{55}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“accharāsaṅghātamattampi ce, bhikkhave, bhikkhu mettācittaṁ manasi karoti;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, if for just the time of a finger snap a bhikkhu attends to a mind of loving-kindness,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave — ‘bhikkhu arittajjhāno viharati satthusāsanakaro ovādapatikaro amoghaṁ raṭṭhapiṇḍaṁ bhuñjati’.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{he is called a bhikkhu who is not devoid of jhāna, who acts upon the teaching of the Teacher, who responds to his advice, and who does not eat the country’s almsfood in vain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ko pana vādo ye naṁ bahulīkarontī”ti! pañcamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{How much more, then, those who cultivate it!” (5)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{56.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{56}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ye keci, bhikkhave, dhammā akusalā akusalabhāgiyā akusalapakkhikā, sabbe te manopubbaṅgamā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, whatever qualities are unwholesome, partake of the unwholesome, and pertain to the unwholesome, all have the mind as their forerunner.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{mano tesaṁ dhammānaṁ paṭhamaṁ uppajjati, anvadeva akusalā dhammā”ti. chaṭṭhaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Mind arises first followed by the unwholesome qualities.” (6)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{57.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{57}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ye keci, bhikkhave, dhammā kusalā kusalabhāgiyā kusalapakkhikā, sabbe te manopubbaṅgamā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, whatever qualities are wholesome, partake of the wholesome, and pertain to the wholesome, all have the mind as their forerunner.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{mano tesaṁ dhammānaṁ paṭhamaṁ uppajjati, anvadeva kusalā dhammā”ti. sattamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Mind arises first followed by the wholesome qualities.” (7)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{58.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{58}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā vā kusalā dhammā parihāyanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, pamādo.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see a single thing that so causes unarisen unwholesome qualities to arise and arisen wholesome qualities to decline as heedlessness.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{pamattassa, bhikkhave, anuppannā ceva akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā ca kusalā dhammā parihāyantī”ti. aṭṭhamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who is heedless, unarisen unwholesome qualities arise and arisen wholesome qualities decline.” (8)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{59.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{59}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā kusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā vā akusalā dhammā parihāyanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, appamādo.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see a single thing that so causes unarisen wholesome qualities to arise and arisen unwholesome qualities to decline as heedfulness.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{appamattassa, bhikkhave, anuppannā ceva kusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā ca akusalā dhammā parihāyantī”ti. navamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who is heedful, unarisen wholesome qualities arise and arisen unwholesome qualities decline.” (9)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{60.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{60}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā vā kusalā dhammā parihāyanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, kosajjaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see a single thing that so causes unarisen unwholesome qualities to arise and arisen wholesome qualities to decline as laziness.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{kusītassa, bhikkhave, anuppannā ceva akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā ca kusalā dhammā parihāyantī”ti. dasamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who is lazy, unarisen unwholesome qualities arise and arisen wholesome qualities decline.” (10)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
{\PaliColumn{accharāsaṅghātavaggo chaṭṭho.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{7. vīriyārambhādivaggo}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{VII. AROUSAL OF ENERGY}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{61.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{61}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā kusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā vā akusalā dhammā parihāyanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, vīriyārambho.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that so causes unarisen wholesome qualities to arise and arisen unwholesome qualities to decline as arousal of energy.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{āraddhavīriyassa, bhikkhave, anuppannā ceva kusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā ca akusalā dhammā parihāyantī”ti. paṭhamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who has aroused energy, unarisen wholesome qualities arise and arisen unwholesome qualities decline.” (1)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{62.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{62}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā vā kusalā dhammā parihāyanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, mahicchatā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that so causes unarisen unwholesome qualities to arise and arisen wholesome qualities to decline as strong desire.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{mahicchassa, bhikkhave, anuppannā ceva akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā ca kusalā dhammā parihāyantī”ti. dutiyaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one with strong desire, unarisen unwholesome qualities arise and arisen wholesome qualities decline.” (2)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{63.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{63}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā kusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā vā akusalā dhammā parihāyanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, appicchatā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that so causes unarisen wholesome qualities to arise and arisen unwholesome qualities to decline as fewness of desires.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{appicchassa, bhikkhave, anuppannā ceva kusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā ca akusalā dhammā parihāyantī”ti. tatiyaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one with few desires, unarisen wholesome qualities arise and arisen unwholesome qualities decline.” (3)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{64.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{64}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā vā kusalā dhammā parihāyanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, asantuṭṭhitā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that so causes unarisen unwholesome qualities to arise and arisen wholesome qualities to decline as non-contentment.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{asantuṭṭhassa, bhikkhave, anuppannā ceva akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā ca kusalā dhammā parihāyantī”ti. catutthaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who is not content, unarisen unwholesome qualities arise and arisen wholesome qualities decline.” (4)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{65.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{65}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā kusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā vā akusalā dhammā parihāyanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, santuṭṭhitā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that so causes unarisen wholesome qualities to arise and arisen unwholesome qualities to decline as contentment.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{santuṭṭhassa, bhikkhave, anuppannā ceva kusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā ca akusalā dhammā parihāyantī”ti. pañcamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who is content, unarisen wholesome qualities arise and arisen unwholesome qualities decline.” (5)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{66.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{66}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā vā kusalā dhammā parihāyanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, ayonisomanasikāro.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that so causes unarisen unwholesome qualities to arise and arisen wholesome qualities to decline as careless attention.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayoniso, bhikkhave, manasi karoto anuppannā ceva akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā ca kusalā dhammā parihāyantī”ti. chaṭṭhaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who attends carelessly, unarisen unwholesome qualities arise and arisen wholesome qualities decline.” (6)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{67.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{67}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā kusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā vā akusalā dhammā parihāyanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, yonisomanasikāro.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that so causes unarisen wholesome qualities to arise and arisen unwholesome qualities to decline as careful attention.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yoniso, bhikkhave, manasi karoto anuppannā ceva kusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā ca akusalā dhammā parihāyantī”ti. sattamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who attends carefully, unarisen wholesome qualities arise and arisen unwholesome qualities decline.” (7)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{68.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{68}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā vā kusalā dhammā parihāyanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, asampajaññaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that so causes unarisen unwholesome qualities to arise and arisen wholesome qualities to decline as lack of clear comprehension.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{asampajānassa, bhikkhave, anuppannā ceva akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā ca kusalā dhammā parihāyantī”ti. aṭṭhamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who does not clearly comprehend, unarisen unwholesome qualities arise and arisen wholesome qualities decline.” (8)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{69.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{69}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā kusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā vā akusalā dhammā parihāyanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, sampajaññaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who clearly comprehends, unarisen wholesome qualities arise and arisen unwholesome qualities decline.” (9)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{70.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{70}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā vā kusalā dhammā parihāyanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, pāpamittatā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that so causes unarisen unwholesome qualities to arise and arisen wholesome qualities to decline as bad friendship.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{pāpamittassa, bhikkhave, anuppannā ceva akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā ca kusalā dhammā parihāyantī”ti. dasamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one with bad friends, unarisen unwholesome qualities arise and arisen wholesome qualities decline.” (10)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
{\PaliColumn{vīriyārambhādivaggo sattamo.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{8. kalyāṇamittādivaggo}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{VIII. GOOD FRIENDSHIP}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{71.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{71}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā kusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā vā akusalā dhammā parihāyanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, kalyāṇamittatā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that so causes unarisen wholesome qualities to arise and arisen unwholesome qualities to decline as good friendship.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{kalyāṇamittassa, bhikkhave, anuppannā ceva kusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā ca akusalā dhammā parihāyantī”ti. paṭhamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one with good friends, unarisen wholesome qualities arise and arisen unwholesome qualities decline.” (1)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{72.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{72}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā vā kusalā dhammā parihāyanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, anuyogo akusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ, ananuyogo kusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that so causes unarisen unwholesome qualities to arise and arisen wholesome qualities to decline as the pursuit of unwholesome qualities and the non-pursuit of wholesome qualities.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{anuyogā, bhikkhave, akusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ, ananuyogā kusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ anuppannā ceva akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā ca kusalā dhammā parihāyantī”ti. dutiyaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Through the pursuit of unwholesome qualities and the non-pursuit of wholesome qualities, unarisen unwholesome qualities arise and arisen wholesome qualities decline.” (2)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{73.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{73}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā kusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā vā akusalā dhammā parihāyanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, anuyogo kusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ, ananuyogo akusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that so causes unarisen wholesome qualities to arise and arisen unwholesome qualities to decline as the pursuit of wholesome qualities and the non-pursuit of unwholesome qualities.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{anuyogā, bhikkhave, kusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ, ananuyogā akusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ anuppannā ceva kusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā ca akusalā dhammā parihāyantī”ti. tatiyaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Through the pursuit of wholesome qualities and the non-pursuit of unwholesome qualities, unarisen wholesome qualities arise and arisen unwholesome qualities decline.” (3)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{74.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{74}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā bojjhaṅgā nuppajjanti uppannā vā bojjhaṅgā na bhāvanāpāripūriṁ gacchanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, ayonisomanasikāro.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that so causes unarisen factors of enlightenment not to arise and arisen factors of enlightenment not to reach fulfillment by development as careless attention.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayoniso, bhikkhave, manasi karoto anuppannā ceva bojjhaṅgā nuppajjanti uppannā ca bojjhaṅgā na bhāvanāpāripūriṁ gacchantī”ti. catutthaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who attends carelessly, unarisen factors of enlightenment do not arise and arisen factors of enlightenment do not reach fulfillment by development.” (4)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{75.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{75}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā bojjhaṅgā uppajjanti uppannā vā bojjhaṅgā bhāvanāpāripūriṁ gacchanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, yonisomanasikāro.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that so causes unarisen factors of enlightenment to arise and arisen factors of enlightenment to reach fulfillment by development as careful attention.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yoniso, bhikkhave, manasi karoto anuppannā ceva bojjhaṅgā uppajjanti uppannā ca bojjhaṅgā bhāvanāpāripūriṁ gacchantī”ti. pañcamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one who attends carefully, unarisen factors of enlightenment arise and arisen factors of enlightenment reach fulfillment by development.” (5)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{76.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{76}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“appamattikā esā, bhikkhave, parihāni yadidaṁ ñātiparihāni.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Insignificant, bhikkhus, is the loss of relatives.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{etaṁ patikiṭṭhaṁ, bhikkhave, parihānīnaṁ yadidaṁ paññāparihānī”ti. chaṭṭhaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The worst thing to lose is wisdom.” (6)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{77.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{77}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“appamattikā esā, bhikkhave, vuddhi yadidaṁ ñātivuddhi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Insignificant, bhikkhus, is the increase of relatives.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{etadaggaṁ, bhikkhave, vuddhīnaṁ yadidaṁ paññāvuddhi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The best thing in which to increase is wisdom.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tasmātiha, bhikkhave, evaṁ sikkhitabbaṁ — ‘paññāvuddhiyā vaddhissāmā’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Therefore, bhikkhus, you should train yourselves thus: ‘We will increase in wisdom.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evañhi vo, bhikkhave, sikkhitabban”ti. sattamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{It is in such a way that you should train yourselves.” (7)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\PaliColumn{kalyāṇamittādivaggo aṭṭhamo.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{9. pamādādivaggo}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{IX. HEEDLESSNESS}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{81.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{81}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“appamattikā esā, bhikkhave, vuddhi yadidaṁ yasovuddhi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Insignificant, bhikkhus, is the increase of fame.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{etadaggaṁ, bhikkhave, vuddhīnaṁ yadidaṁ paññāvuddhi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The best thing in which to increase is wisdom.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tasmātiha, bhikkhave, evaṁ sikkhitabbaṁ — ‘paññāvuddhiyā vaddhissāmā’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Therefore, bhikkhus, you should train yourselves thus: ‘We will increase in wisdom.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evañhi vo, bhikkhave, sikkhitabban”ti. paṭhamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{It is in such a way that you should train yourselves.” (1)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{82.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{82}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yo evaṁ mahato anatthāya saṁvattati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, pamādo.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that leads to such great harm as heedlessness.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{pamādo, bhikkhave, mahato anatthāya saṁvattatī”ti. dutiyaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Heedlessness leads to great harm.” (2)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{83.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{83}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yo evaṁ mahato atthāya saṁvattati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, appamādo.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that leads to such great good as heedfulness.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{appamādo, bhikkhave, mahato atthāya saṁvattatī”ti. tatiyaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Heedfulness leads to great good.” (3)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{84.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{84}}\\
\end{addmargin}

{\PaliColumn{yonisomanasikāro, bhikkhave, saddhammassa ṭhitiyā asammosāya anantaradhānāya saṁvattatī”ti. chabbīsatimaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Careful attention leads the continuation, non-decline, and non-disappearance of the good Dhamma.” (26)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{124.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{124}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yo evaṁ saddhammassa sammosāya antaradhānāya saṁvattati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, asampajaññaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that so leads to the decline and disappearance of the good Dhamma as lack of clear comprehension.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{asampajaññaṁ, bhikkhave, saddhammassa ṭhitiyā asammosāya anantaradhānāya saṁvattatī”ti. sattavīsatimaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Lack of clear comprehension leads to the decline and disappearance of the good Dhamma.” (27)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{126.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{126}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yo evaṁ saddhammassa sammosāya antaradhānāya saṁvattati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, pāpamittatā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Among external factors, bhikkhus, I do not see even a single factor that leads to such great harm as bad friendship.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{pāpamittatā, bhikkhave, saddhammassa ṭhitiyā asammosāya anantaradhānāya saṁvattatī”ti. ekūnatiṁsatimaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Bad friendship leads to the decline and disappearance of the good Dhamma.” (29)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{127.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yo evaṁ saddhammassa ṭhitiyā asammosāya anantaradhānāya saṁvattati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, kalyāṇamittatā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{128.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{128}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yo evaṁ saddhammassa sammosāya antaradhānāya saṁvattati yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, anuyogo akusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ, ananuyogo kusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing that so leads to the decline and disappearance of the good Dhamma as the pursuit of unwholesome qualities and the non-pursuit of wholesome qualities.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{anuyogo, bhikkhave, akusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ, ananuyogo kusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ saddhammassa sammosāya antaradhānāya saṁvattatī”ti. ekattiṁsatimaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The pursuit of unwholesome qualities and the non-pursuit of wholesome qualitiesleads to the decline and disappearance of the good Dhamma.” (31)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The pursuit of wholesome qualities and the non-pursuit of unwholesome qualities leads the continuation, non-decline, and non-disappearance of the good Dhamma.” (32)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{130.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{130}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ye te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū adhammaṁ dhammoti dīpenti te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū bahujanāhitāya paṭipannā bahujanāsukhāya, bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, those bhikkhus who explain non-Dhamma as Dhamma are acting for the harm of many people, the unhappiness of many people, for the ruin, harm, and suffering of many people, of devas and human beings.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{bahuñca te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū apuññaṁ pasavanti, te cimaṁ saddhammaṁ antaradhāpentī”ti. tettiṁsatimaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{These bhikkhus generate much demerit and cause this good Dhamma to disappear.” (33)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\PaliColumn{dutiyapamādādivaggo dasamo.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{11. adhammavaggo}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{XI. NON-DHAMMA}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{140.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{140}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ye te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū adhammaṁ adhammoti dīpenti te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū bahujanahitāya paṭipannā bahujanasukhāya, bahuno janassa atthāya hitāya sukhāya devamanussānaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, those bhikkhus who explain non-Dhamma as non-Dhamma are acting for the welfare of many people, for the happiness of many people, for the good, welfare, and happiness of many people, of devas and human beings.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{bahuñca te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū puññaṁ pasavanti, te cimaṁ saddhammaṁ ṭhapentī”ti. paṭhamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{These bhikkhus generate much merit and sustain this good Dhamma.” (1)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{141.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{141}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ye te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū dhammaṁ dhammoti dīpenti te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū bahujanahitāya paṭipannā bahujanasukhāya, bahuno janassa atthāya hitāya sukhāya devamanussānaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, those bhikkhus who explain Dhamma as Dhamma are acting for the welfare of many people, for the happiness of many people, for the good, welfare, and happiness of many people, of devas and human beings.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{bahuñca te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū puññaṁ pasavanti, te cimaṁ saddhammaṁ ṭhapentī”ti. dutiyaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{These bhikkhus generate much merit and sustain this good Dhamma.” (2)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\EnglishColumn{These bhikkhus generate much merit and sustain this good Dhamma.” (10)}}\\

{\PaliColumn{adhammavaggo ekādasamo.}}\\

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{12. anāpattivaggo}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{XII. NOT AN OFFENSE}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{150.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{150}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ye te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū anāpattiṁ āpattīti dīpenti te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū bahujanāhitāya paṭipannā bahujanāsukhāya, bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, those bhikkhus who explain what is not an offense as an offense are acting for the harm of many people, for the unhappiness of many people, for the ruin, harm, and suffering of many people, of devas and human beings.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{bahuñca te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū apuññaṁ pasavanti, te cimaṁ saddhammaṁ antaradhāpentī”ti. paṭhamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{These bhikkhus generate much demerit and cause this good Dhamma to disappear.” (1)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{151.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{151}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ye te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū āpattiṁ anāpattīti dīpenti te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū bahujanāhitāya paṭipannā bahujanāsukhāya, bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, those bhikkhus who explain what is an offense as no offense are acting for the harm of many people, for the unhappiness of many people, for the ruin, harm, and suffering of many people, of devas and human beings.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{bahuñca te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū apuññaṁ pasavanti, te cimaṁ saddhammaṁ antaradhāpentī”ti. dutiyaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{These bhikkhus generate much demerit and cause this good Dhamma to disappear.” (2)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{152.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{152}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ye te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū lahukaṁ āpattiṁ garukā āpattīti dīpenti te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū bahujanāhitāya paṭipannā bahujanāsukhāya, bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, those bhikkhus who explain what is a light offense as a grave offense are acting for the harm of many people, for the unhappiness of many people, for the ruin, harm, and suffering of many people, of devas and human beings.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{bahuñca te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū apuññaṁ pasavanti, te cimaṁ saddhammaṁ antaradhāpentī”ti. tatiyaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{These bhikkhus generate much demerit and cause this good Dhamma to disappear.” (3)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{153.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{153}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{154}}\\
\end{addmargin}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

{\EnglishColumn{155}}\\
\end{addmargin}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{156.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{156}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ye te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū sāvasesaṁ āpattiṁ anavasesā āpattīti dīpenti te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū bahujanāhitāya paṭipannā bahujanāsukhāya, bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaṁ.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
