\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{157.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{157}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ye te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū anavasesaṁ āpattiṁ sāvasesā āpattīti dīpenti te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū bahujanāhitāya paṭipannā bahujanāsukhāya, bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, those bhikkhus who explain what is an irremediable offense as a remediable offense are acting for the harm of many people, for the unhappiness of many people, for the ruin, harm, and suffering of many people, of devas and human beings.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{bahuñca te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū apuññaṁ pasavanti, te cimaṁ saddhammaṁ antaradhāpentī”ti. aṭṭhamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{These bhikkhus generate much demerit and cause this good Dhamma to disappear.” (8)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{158.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{158}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ye te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū sappaṭikammaṁ āpattiṁ appaṭikammā āpattīti dīpenti te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū bahujanāhitāya paṭipannā bahujanāsukhāya, bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, those bhikkhus who explain what is an offense with redress as an offense without redress are acting for the harm of many people, for the unhappiness of many people, for the ruin, harm, and suffering of many people, of devas and human beings.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{These bhikkhus generate much demerit and cause this good Dhamma to disappear.” (9)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
{\PaliColumn{anāpattivaggo dvādasamo.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{  13. ekapuggalavaggo}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{XIII. ONE PERSON}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{170.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{170}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ekapuggalo, bhikkhave, loke uppajjamāno uppajjati bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya lokānukampāya atthāya hitāya sukhāya devamanussānaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, there is one person who arises in the world for the welfare of many people, for the happiness of many people, out of compassion for the world, for the good, welfare, and happiness of devas and human beings.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{katamo ekapuggalo?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Who is that one person?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tathāgato arahaṁ sammāsambuddho.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The Tathāgata, the Arahant, the Perfectly Enlightened One.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṁ kho, bhikkhave, ekapuggalo loke uppajjamāno uppajjati bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya lokānukampāya atthāya hitāya sukhāya devamanussānan”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{This is that one person who arises in the world for the welfare of many people, for the happiness of many people, out of compassion for the world, for the good, welfare, and happiness of devas and human beings.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{171.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{171}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ekapuggalassa, bhikkhave, pātubhāvo dullabho lokasmiṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, the manifestation of one person is rare in the world.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{katamassa ekapuggalassa?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Who is that one person?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tathāgatassa arahato sammāsambuddhassa.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The Tathāgata, the Arahant, the Perfectly Enlightened One.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{imassa kho, bhikkhave, ekapuggalassa pātubhāvo dullabho lokasmin”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{This is the manifestation of one person that is rare in the world.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{172.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{172}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ekapuggalo, bhikkhave, loke uppajjamāno uppajjati acchariyamanusso.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, there is one person arising in the world who is extraordinary.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{katamo ekapuggalo?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Who is that one person?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tathāgato arahaṁ sammāsambuddho.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The Tathāgata, the Arahant, the Perfectly Enlightened One.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṁ kho, bhikkhave, ekapuggalo loke uppajjamāno uppajjati acchariyamanusso”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{This is one person arising in the world who is extraordinary.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{173.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{173}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ekapuggalassa, bhikkhave, kālakiriyā bahuno janassa anutappā hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, the death of one person is lamented by many people.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{katamassa ekapuggalassa?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Who is that one person?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tathāgatassa arahato sammāsambuddhassa.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The Tathāgata, the Arahant, the Perfectly Enlightened One.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{imassa kho, bhikkhave, ekapuggalassa kālakiriyā bahuno janassa anutappā hotī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{This is the death of one person that is lamented by many people.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ekapuggalo, bhikkhave, loke uppajjamāno uppajjati adutiyo asahāyo appaṭimo appaṭisamo appaṭibhāgo appaṭipuggalo asamo asamasamo dvipadānaṁ aggo.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, there is one person arising in the world who is unique, without a peer, without counterpart, incomparable, matchless, unrivaled, unequaled, without equal, the foremost of bipeds.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{katamo ekapuggalo?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Who is that one person?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The Tathāgata, the Arahant, the Perfectly Enlightened One.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṁ kho, bhikkhave, ekapuggalo loke uppajjamāno uppajjati adutiyo asahāyo appaṭimo appaṭisamo appaṭibhāgo appaṭipuggalo asamo asamasamo dvipadānaṁ aggo”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{This is that one person arising in the world who is unique, without a peer, without counterpart, incomparable, matchless, unrivaled, unequaled, without equal, the foremost of bipeds.”}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekapuggalampi samanupassāmi yo evaṁ tathāgatena anuttaraṁ dhammacakkaṁ pavattitaṁ sammadeva anuppavatteti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, sāriputto.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single person who properly continues to keep in motion the unsurpassed wheel of the Dhamma set in motion by the Tathāgata as does Sāriputta.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{sāriputto, bhikkhave, tathāgatena anuttaraṁ dhammacakkaṁ pavattitaṁ sammadeva anuppavattetī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Sāriputta properly continues to keep in motion the unsurpassed wheel of the Dhamma set in motion by the Tathāgata.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
{\PaliColumn{ekapuggalavaggo terasamo.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{14. etadaggavaggo}}\\

{\PaliColumn{15. aṭṭhānapāḷi}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{XV. IMPOSSIBLE}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\PaliColumn{1. paṭhamavaggo (AN 1.268-277)}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{268.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{268}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“aṭṭhānametaṁ, bhikkhave, anavakāso yaṁ diṭṭhisampanno puggalo kañci saṅkhāraṁ niccato upagaccheyya.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“It is impossible and inconceivable, bhikkhus, that a person accomplished in view could consider any conditioned phenomenon as permanent;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{netaṁ ṭhānaṁ vijjati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{there is no such possibility.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ṭhānañca kho etaṁ, bhikkhave, vijjati yaṁ puthujjano kañci saṅkhāraṁ niccato upagaccheyya.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{But it is possible that a worldling might consider some conditioned phenomenon as permanent;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ṭhānametaṁ vijjatī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{there is such a possibility.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{269.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{269}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“It is impossible and inconceivable, bhikkhus, that a person accomplished in view could consider any conditioned phenomenon as pleasurable;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\setstretch{.7}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\PaliColumn{ṭhānañca kho etaṁ, bhikkhave, vijjati yaṁ puthujjano tathāgatassa paduṭṭhacitto lohitaṁ uppādeyya.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{But it is possible that a worldling might, with a mind of hatred, shed the blood of the Tathāgatha;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ṭhānametaṁ vijjatī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{there is such a possibility.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\setstretch{.7}

\end{addmargin}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

{\EnglishColumn{there is such a possibility.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}

\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“aṭṭhānametaṁ, bhikkhave, anavakāso yaṁ vacīsucaritassa aniṭṭho akanto amanāpo vipāko nibbatteyya.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“It is impossible and inconceivable, bhikkhus, that an unwished for, undesired, disagreeable result could be produced from verbal good conduct;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{netaṁ ṭhānaṁ vijjati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{there is no such possibility.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ṭhānañca kho etaṁ, bhikkhave, vijjati yaṁ vacīsucaritassa iṭṭho kanto manāpo vipāko nibbatteyya.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{But it is possible that a wished for, desired, agreeable result could be produced from verbal good conduct;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ṭhānametaṁ vijjatī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{there is such a possibility.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{289.}}\\

{\PaliColumn{290.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{290}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“aṭṭhānametaṁ, bhikkhave, anavakāso yaṁ kāyaduccaritasamaṅgī tannidānā tappaccayā kāyassa bhedā paraṁ maraṇā sugatiṁ saggaṁ lokaṁ upapajjeyya.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“It is impossible and inconceivable, bhikkhus, that a person engaging in bodily misconduct could on that account, for that reason, with the breakup of the body, after death, be reborn in a good destination, in a heavenly world;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{netaṁ ṭhānaṁ vijjati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{But it is possible that a person engaging in bodily misconduct could on that account, for that reason, with the breakup of the body, after death, be reborn in the plane of misery, in a bad destination, in the lower world, in hell;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{16. ekadhammapāḷi}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{XVI. ONE THING}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{1. paṭhamavaggo (AN 1.296-297)}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{i. First Subchapter}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{296.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{296}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ekadhammo, bhikkhave, bhāvito bahulīkato ekantanibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya upasamāya abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṁvattati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, there is one thing that, when developed and cultivated, leads exclusively to disenchantment, to dispassion, to cessation, to peace, to direct knowledge, to enlightenment, to nibbāna.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{katamo ekadhammo?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{What is that one thing?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{buddhānussati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Recollection of the Buddha.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṁ kho, bhikkhave, ekadhammo bhāvito bahulīkato ekantanibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya upasamāya abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṁvattatī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{This is that one thing that, when developed and cultivated, leads exclusively to disenchantment, to dispassion, to cessation, to peace, to direct knowledge, to enlightenment, to nibbāna.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

{\PaliColumn{2. dutiyavaggo (AN 1.298-307)}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{ii. Second Subchapter}}\\

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{298.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{306}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena anuppannā vā akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā vā akusalā dhammā bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saṁvattanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, micchādiṭṭhi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing on account of which unarisen unwholesome qualities arise and arisen unwholesome qualities increase and expand so much as wrong view.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{micchādiṭṭhikassa, bhikkhave, anuppannā ceva akusalā dhammā uppajjanti uppannā ca akusalā dhammā bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saṁvattantī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For one of wrong view, unarisen unwholesome qualities arise and arisen unwholesome qualities increase and expand.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{304.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{312}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena sattā kāyassa bhedā paraṁ maraṇā apāyaṁ duggatiṁ vinipātaṁ nirayaṁ upapajjanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, micchādiṭṭhi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing on account of which, with the breakup of the body, after death, beings are reborn in the plane of misery, in a bad destination, in the lower world, in hell, so much as wrong view.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{micchādiṭṭhiyā, bhikkhave, samannāgatā sattā kāyassa bhedā paraṁ maraṇā apāyaṁ duggatiṁ vinipātaṁ nirayaṁ upapajjantī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Possessing wrong view, with the breakup of the body, after death, beings are reborn in the plane of misery, in a bad destination, in the lower world, in hell.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{305.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{313}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yena sattā kāyassa bhedā paraṁ maraṇā sugatiṁ saggaṁ lokaṁ upapajjanti yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, sammādiṭṭhi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing on account of which, with the breakup of the body, after death, beings are reborn in a good destination, in a heavenly world, so much as right view.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{sammādiṭṭhiyā, bhikkhave, samannāgatā sattā kāyassa bhedā paraṁ maraṇā sugatiṁ saggaṁ lokaṁ upapajjantī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Possessing right view, with the breakup of the body, after death, beings are reborn in a good destination, in a heavenly world.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{306.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{314}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“micchādiṭṭhikassa, bhikkhave, purisapuggalassa yañceva kāyakammaṁ yathādiṭṭhi samattaṁ samādinnaṁ yañca vacīkammaṁ yathādiṭṭhi samattaṁ samādinnaṁ yañca manokammaṁ yathādiṭṭhi samattaṁ samādinnaṁ}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, for a person of wrong view, whatever bodily kamma, verbal kamma, and mental kamma he instigates and undertakes in accordance with that view,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yā ca cetanā yā ca patthanā yo ca paṇidhi ye ca saṅkhārā sabbe te dhammā aniṭṭhāya akantāya amanāpāya ahitāya dukkhāya saṁvattanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and whatever his volition, yearning, inclination, and volitional activities, all lead to what is unwished for, undesired, and disagreeable, to harm and suffering.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{diṭṭhi hissa, bhikkhave, pāpikā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Because the view is bad.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, nimbabījaṁ vā kosātakibījaṁ vā tittakalābubījaṁ vā allāya pathaviyā nikkhittaṁ}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Suppose, bhikkhus, a seed of neem, bitter cucumber, or bitter gourd were planted in moist soil.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yañceva pathavirasaṁ upādiyati yañca āporasaṁ upādiyati sabbaṁ taṁ tittakattāya kaṭukattāya asātattāya saṁvattati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Whatever nutrients it takes up from the soil and from the water would all lead to its bitter, pungent, and disagreeable flavor.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{bījaṁ hissa, bhikkhave, pāpakaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Because the seed is bad.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evamevaṁ kho, bhikkhave, micchādiṭṭhikassa purisapuggalassa yañceva kāyakammaṁ yathādiṭṭhi samattaṁ samādinnaṁ yañca vacīkammaṁ yathādiṭṭhi samattaṁ samādinnaṁ yañca manokammaṁ yathādiṭṭhi samattaṁ samādinnaṁ}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{So too, for a person of wrong view, whatever bodily kamma, verbal kamma, and mental kamma he instigates and undertakes in accordance with that view,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yā ca cetanā yā ca patthanā yo ca paṇidhi ye ca saṅkhārā sabbe te dhammā aniṭṭhāya akantāya amanāpāya ahitāya dukkhāya saṁvattanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and whatever his volition, yearning, inclination, and volitional activities, all lead to what is unwished for, undesired, and disagreeable, to harm and suffering.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{diṭṭhi hissa, bhikkhave, pāpikā”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Because the view is bad.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{307.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{315}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“sammādiṭṭhikassa, bhikkhave, purisapuggalassa yañceva kāyakammaṁ yathādiṭṭhi samattaṁ samādinnaṁ yañca vacīkammaṁ yathādiṭṭhi samattaṁ samādinnaṁ yañca manokammaṁ yathādiṭṭhi samattaṁ samādinnaṁ}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, for a person of right view, whatever bodily kamma, verbal kamma, and mental kamma he instigates and undertakes in accordance with that view,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yā ca cetanā yā ca patthanā yo ca paṇidhi ye ca saṅkhārā sabbe te dhammā iṭṭhāya kantāya manāpāya hitāya sukhāya saṁvattanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and whatever his volition, yearning, inclination, and volitional activities, all lead to what is wished for, desired, and agreeable, to well-being and happiness.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{diṭṭhi hissa, bhikkhave, bhaddikā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Because the view is good.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, ucchubījaṁ vā sālibījaṁ vā muddikābījaṁ vā allāya pathaviyā nikkhittaṁ}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Suppose, bhikkhus, a seed of sugar cane, hill rice, or grape were planted in moist soil.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yañceva pathavirasaṁ upādiyati yañca āporasaṁ upādiyati sabbaṁ taṁ madhurattāya sātattāya asecanakattāya saṁvattati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Whatever nutrients it takes up from the soil and from the water would all lead to its sweet, agreeable, and delectable flavor.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{bījaṁ hissa, bhikkhave, bhaddakaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Because the seed is good.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evamevaṁ kho, bhikkhave, sammādiṭṭhikassa purisapuggalassa yañceva kāyakammaṁ yathādiṭṭhi samattaṁ samādinnaṁ yañca vacīkammaṁ yathādiṭṭhi samattaṁ samādinnaṁ yañca manokammaṁ yathādiṭṭhi samattaṁ samādinnaṁ}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{So too, for a person of right view, whatever bodily kamma, verbal kamma, and mental kamma he instigates and undertakes in accordance with that view,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yā ca cetanā yā ca patthanā yo ca paṇidhi ye ca saṅkhārā sabbe te dhammā iṭṭhāya kantāya manāpāya hitāya sukhāya saṁvattanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and whatever his volition, yearning, inclination, and volitional activities, all lead to what is wished for, desired, and agreeable, to welfare and happiness.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{diṭṭhi hissa, bhikkhave, bhaddikā”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Because the view is good.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
{\PaliColumn{vaggo dutiyo.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{3. tatiyavaggo (AN 1.308-321)}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{iii. Third Subchapter}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{308.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{316}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ekapuggalo, bhikkhave, loke uppajjamāno uppajjati bahujanāhitāya bahujanāsukhāya, bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, there is one person who arises in the world for the harm of many people, for the unhappiness of many people, for the ruin, harm, and suffering of many people, of devas and human beings.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{katamo ekapuggalo?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Who is that one person?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{micchādiṭṭhiko hoti viparītadassano.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{It is one who holds wrong view and has an incorrect perspective.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so bahujanaṁ saddhammā vuṭṭhāpetvā asaddhamme patiṭṭhāpeti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{He draws many people away from the good Dhamma and establishes them in a bad Dhamma.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṁ kho, bhikkhave, ekapuggalo loke uppajjamāno uppajjati bahujanāhitāya bahujanāsukhāya, bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānan”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{This is that one person who arises in the world for the harm of many people, the unhappiness of many people, for the ruin, harm, and suffering of many people, of devas and human beings.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{309.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{317}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ekapuggalo, bhikkhave, loke uppajjamāno uppajjati bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya, bahuno janassa atthāya hitāya sukhāya devamanussānaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, there is one person who arises in the world for the welfare of many people, for the happiness of many people, for the good, welfare, and happiness of many people, of devas and human beings.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{katamo ekapuggalo?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Who is that one person?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{sammādiṭṭhiko hoti aviparītadassano.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{It is one who holds right view and has a correct perspective.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so bahujanaṁ asaddhammā vuṭṭhāpetvā saddhamme patiṭṭhāpeti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{He draws many people away from a bad Dhamma and establishes them in the good Dhamma.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṁ kho, bhikkhave, ekapuggalo loke upapajjamāno uppajjati bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya, bahuno janassa atthāya hitāya sukhāya devamanussānan”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{This is that one person who arises in the world for the welfare of many people, for the happiness of many people, for the good, welfare, and happiness of many people, of devas and human beings.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{310.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{318}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yaṁ evaṁ mahāsāvajjaṁ yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, micchādiṭṭhi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single thing so blameworthy as wrong view.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{micchādiṭṭhiparamāni, bhikkhave, mahāsāvajjānī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Wrong view is the worst of things that are blameworthy.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{311.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{319}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, aññaṁ ekapuggalampi samanupassāmi yo evaṁ bahujanāhitāya paṭipanno bahujanāsukhāya, bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaṁ yathayidaṁ, bhikkhave, makkhali moghapuriso.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, I do not see even a single person who is acting so much for the harm of many people, the unhappiness of many people, for the ruin, harm, and suffering of many people, of devas and human beings, as the hollow man Makkhali.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, nadīmukhe khippaṁ uḍḍeyya bahūnaṁ macchānaṁ ahitāya dukkhāya anayāya byasanāya;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Just as a trap set at the mouth of a river would bring about harm, suffering, calamity, and disaster for many fish,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evamevaṁ kho, bhikkhave, makkhali moghapuriso manussakhippaṁ maññe loke uppanno bahūnaṁ sattānaṁ ahitāya dukkhāya anayāya byasanāyā”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{so too, the hollow man Makkhali is, as it were, a ‘trap for people’ who has arisen in the world for the harm, suffering, calamity, and disaster of many beings.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{312.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{320}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“durakkhāte, bhikkhave, dhammavinaye yo ca samādapeti yañca samādapeti yo ca samādapito tathattāya paṭipajjati sabbe te bahuṁ apuññaṁ pasavanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, one who encourages [others] in a badly expounded Dhamma and discipline, and the one whom he encourages, and the one who, thus encouraged, practices in accordance with it, all generate much demerit.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{durakkhātattā, bhikkhave, dhammassā”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Because that Dhamma is badly expounded.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{313.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{321}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“svākkhāte, bhikkhave, dhammavinaye yo ca samādapeti yañca samādapeti yo ca samādapito tathattāya paṭipajjati sabbe te bahuṁ puññaṁ pasavanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, one who encourages [others] in a well-expounded Dhamma and discipline, and the one whom he encourages, and the one who, thus encouraged, practices in accordance with it, all generate much merit.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{svākkhātattā, bhikkhave, dhammassā”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Because that Dhamma is well expounded.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{314.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{322}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“durakkhāte, bhikkhave, dhammavinaye dāyakena mattā jānitabbā, no paṭiggāhakena.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, with a badly expounded Dhamma and discipline, moderation should be known by the giver [of a gift], not by the recipient.}}\\

\setstretch{.5}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{316.}}\\

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Because that Dhamma is badly expounded.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{317.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{325}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“svākkhāte, bhikkhave, dhammavinaye yo kusīto so dukkhaṁ viharati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, whoever is lazy in a well-expounded Dhamma and discipline dwells in suffering.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṁ kissa hetu?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For what reason?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{svākkhātattā, bhikkhave, dhammassā”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Because that Dhamma is well expounded.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{318.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{326}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“durakkhāte, bhikkhave, dhammavinaye yo kusīto so sukhaṁ viharati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{320.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{328}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, appamattakopi gūtho duggandho hoti;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, just as even a trifling amount of feces is foul smelling,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evamevaṁ kho ahaṁ, bhikkhave, appamattakampi bhavaṁ na vaṇṇemi, antamaso accharāsaṅghātamattampi”.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{so too I do not praise even a trifling amount of existence, even for a mere finger snap.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\PaliColumn{vaggo tatiyo.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{4. catutthavaggo (AN 1.322-363-365)}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{iv. Jambudīpa Repetition Series [Fourth Subchapter]}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{322.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{333}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, appamattakaṁ imasmiṁ jambudīpe ārāmarāmaṇeyyakaṁ vanarāmaṇeyyakaṁ bhūmirāmaṇeyyakaṁ pokkharaṇirāmaṇeyyakaṁ;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Just as, bhikkhus, in this Jambudīpa, delightful parks, groves, landscapes, and lotus ponds are few,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{atha kho etadeva bahutaraṁ yadidaṁ ukkūlavikūlaṁ nadīviduggaṁ khāṇukaṇṭakaṭṭhānaṁ pabbatavisamaṁ;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{while more numerous are the hills and slopes, rivers that are hard to cross, places with stumps and thorns, and rugged mountains,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evamevaṁ kho, bhikkhave, appakā te sattā ye thalajā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{so too those beings are few who are born on dry ground;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{atha kho eteva sattā bahutarā ye odakā”.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{more numerous are those beings who are born in water.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{335. “...}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{347 “...}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evamevaṁ kho, bhikkhave, appakā te sattā ye attharasassa dhammarasassa vimuttirasassa lābhino;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{so too those beings are few who obtain the taste of the meaning, the taste of the Dhamma, the taste of liberation;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{atha kho eteva sattā bahutarā ye attharasassa dhammarasassa vimuttirasassa na lābhino.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{more numerous are those who do not obtain the taste of the meaning, the taste of the Dhamma, the taste of liberation.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tasmātiha, bhikkhave, evaṁ sikkhitabbaṁ —}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Therefore, bhikkhus, you should train yourselves thus:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{attharasassa dhammarasassa vimuttirasassa lābhino bhavissāmāti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘We will obtain the taste of the meaning, the taste of the Dhamma, the taste of liberation.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evañhi vo, bhikkhave, sikkhitabbanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{It is in such a way that you should train yourselves.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{336.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{348}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, appamattakaṁ imasmiṁ jambudīpe ārāmarāmaṇeyyakaṁ vanarāmaṇeyyakaṁ bhūmirāmaṇeyyakaṁ pokkharaṇirāmaṇeyyakaṁ;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Just as, bhikkhus, in this Jambudīpa delightful parks, groves, landscapes, and lotus ponds are few,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{atha kho etadeva bahutaraṁ yadidaṁ ukkūlavikūlaṁ nadīviduggaṁ khāṇukaṇṭakaṭṭhānaṁ pabbatavisamaṁ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{while more numerous are the hills and slopes, rivers that are hard to cross, places with stumps and thorns, and rugged mountains,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evamevaṁ kho, bhikkhave, appakā te sattā ye manussā cutā manussesu paccājāyanti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{so too those beings are few who, when they pass away as human beings, are reborn among human beings.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{atha kho eteva sattā bahutarā ye manussā cutā niraye paccājāyanti.”}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{More numerous are those who, when they pass away as human beings, are reborn in hell.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\PaliColumn{atha kho eteva sattā bahutarā ye nirayā cutā pettivisaye paccājāyanti.”}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{More numerous are those who, when they pass away from hell, are reborn in the sphere of afflicted spirits.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{so too those beings are few who, when they pass away from the animal realm, are reborn among human beings.}}\\
\end{addmargin}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{17. pasādakaradhammavaggo}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{XVII. QUALITIES ENGENDERING CONFIDENCE}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{378}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“addhamidaṁ, bhikkhave, lābhānaṁ yadidaṁ āraññikattaṁ.”}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, this is certainly a type of gain, namely, being a forest-dweller.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\setstretch{.7}

\setstretch{.5}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, this is certainly a type of gain, namely, having good health.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
{\PaliColumn{soḷasa pasādakaradhammā niṭṭhitā.}}\\

{\PaliColumn{pasādakaradhammavaggo sattarasamo.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{  18. aparāccharāsaṅghātavaggo}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{XVIII. FINGER SNAP}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{382.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{394}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“accharāsaṅghātamattampi ce, bhikkhave, bhikkhu paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ bhāveti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, if for just the time of a finger snap a bhikkhu develops the first jhāna,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{he is called}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘bhikkhu arittajjhāno viharati, satthusāsanakaro ovādapatikaro, amoghaṁ raṭṭhapiṇḍaṁ bhuñjati.’}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{a bhikkhu who is not devoid of jhāna, who acts upon the teaching of the Teacher, who responds to his advice, and who does not eat the country’s almsfood in vain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ko pana vādo ye naṁ bahulīkarontī”ti!}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{How much more, then, those who cultivate it!”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{394-397.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{(406) generates desire for the non-arising of unarisen bad unwholesome qualities; makes an effort, arouses energy, applies his mind, and strives ...}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{anuppannānaṁ pāpakānaṁ akusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ anuppādāya chandaṁ janeti vāyamati vīriyaṁ ārabhati cittaṁ paggaṇhāti padahati; uppannānaṁ pāpakānaṁ akusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ pahānāya chandaṁ janeti vāyamati vīriyaṁ ārabhati cittaṁ paggaṇhāti padahati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{(407) generates desire for the abandoning of arisen bad unwholesome qualities; makes an effort, arouses energy, applies his mind, and strives ...}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

{\EnglishColumn{What is that one thing?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

{\EnglishColumn{Mindfulness directed to the body.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{This is the one thing that, when developed and cultivated, leads to penetrativeness of wisdom.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{vijjāvimuttiphalasacchikiriyāya saṁvattatī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{THE DEATHLESS}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{571. “ekadhamme, bhikkhave, bhāvite bahulīkate kāyopi passambhati, cittampi passambhati, vitakkavicārāpi vūpasammanti, kevalāpi vijjābhāgiyā dhammā bhāvanāpāripūriṁ gacchanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{616}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{katamasmiṁ ekadhamme?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, they do not partake of the deathless who do not partake of mindfulness directed to the body.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{kāyagatāya satiyā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{They partake of the deathless who partake of mindfulness directed to the body.” (1)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\PaliColumn{imasmiṁ kho, bhikkhave, ekadhamme bhāvite bahulīkate kāyopi passambhati, cittampi passambhati, vitakkavicārāpi vūpasammanti, kevalāpi vijjābhāgiyā dhammā bhāvanāpāripūriṁ gacchantī”ti.}}\\

{\EnglishColumn{617}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{572. “ekadhamme, bhikkhave, bhāvite bahulīkate anuppannā ceva akusalā dhammā nuppajjanti, uppannā ca akusalā dhammā pahīyanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, the deathless has not been partaken of by those who have not partaken of mindfulness directed to the body.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{katamasmiṁ ekadhamme?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The deathless has been partaken of by those who have partaken of mindfulness directed to the body.” (2)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\PaliColumn{kāyagatāya satiyā.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{imasmiṁ kho, bhikkhave, ekadhamme bhāvite bahulīkate anuppannā ceva akusalā dhammā nuppajjanti, uppannā ca akusalā dhammā pahīyantī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{618}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, they have fallen away from the deathless who have fallen away from mindfulness directed to the body.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{573. “ekadhamme, bhikkhave, bhāvite bahulīkate anuppannā ceva kusalā dhammā uppajjanti, uppannā ca kusalā dhammā bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saṁvattanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{They have not fallen away from the deathless who have not fallen away from mindfulness directed to the body.” (3)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\PaliColumn{katamasmiṁ ekadhamme?}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{kāyagatāya satiyā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{619}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{imasmiṁ kho, bhikkhave, ekadhamme bhāvite bahulīkate anuppannā ceva kusalā dhammā uppajjanti, uppannā ca kusalā dhammā bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya saṁvattantī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, they have neglected the deathless who have neglected mindfulness directed to the body.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\EnglishColumn{They have undertaken the deathless who have undertaken mindfulness directed to the body.” (4)}}\\

{\PaliColumn{574. “ekadhamme, bhikkhave, bhāvite bahulīkate avijjā pahīyati, vijjā uppajjati, asmimāno pahīyati, anusayā samugghātaṁ gacchanti, saṁyojanā pahīyanti.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{katamasmiṁ ekadhamme?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{620}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{kāyagatāya satiyā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Bhikkhus, they are heedless about the deathless who are heedless about mindfulness directed to the body.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{imasmiṁ kho, bhikkhave, ekadhamme bhāvite bahulīkate avijjā pahīyati, vijjā uppajjati, asmimāno pahīyati, anusayā samugghātaṁ gacchanti, saṁyojanā pahīyantī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{They are not heedless about the deathless who are not heedless about mindfulness directed to the body.” (5)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
